GT Equivalence Verification (CRK20)

GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_p*sin(c3*A)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function of two variables \(t,A\):
\[
f(t,A)= -0.3122128845632889\,A\,e^{-0.07984001873836775\,t}\;+\;0.4717280564351947\,\sin(0.8721876285304352\,A).
\]
So any matching candidate must be expressible as
- one term of the form \((\text{constant})\cdot A\cdot e^{(\text{constant})t}\) with **no other \(t\)-dependence**, plus
- one term of the form \((\text{constant})\cdot \sin((\text{constant})A)\) with **no phase shift**, and
- **no extra additive constants** or other \(A\)/\(t\) terms (unless their coefficients can be set to 0).

Also note: the GT sine term has **zero phase** (no “+ b” inside sine), and the exponential term has a **negative** exponent coefficient.

---

### 1. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + c2\sin(A c3 + c4) + c5\)
Set \(c5=0\). Need \(\sin(Ac3+c4)=\sin(kA)\) for all \(A\), which forces \(c4=0\) (mod \(2\pi\)); choose \(c4=0\). Then match coefficients:
- \(c0=-0.3122128845632889\)
- \(c1=-0.07984001873836775\)
- \(c2=0.4717280564351947\)
- \(c3=0.8721876285304352\)
Works. ✅

### 2. Candidate 1 plus extra \(c6 t^{c7} e^{c8 t}\log(Ac9+1)\)
Set \(c6=0\) to remove the extra term, then reduce to Candidate 1, which can match as above. ✅

### 3. \(c0\sin(Ac1+c2)+c3 e^{c4 t}\max(0,A)\)
The GT has \(A e^{kt}\) for **all real \(A\)**, but \(\max(0,A)\) is 0 for \(A<0\). No parameter choice makes \(\max(0,A)\) equal to \(A\) for all \(A\). ❌

### 4. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + c2\sin(A c3 + c4)\)
Need zero phase: set \(c4=0\) (mod \(2\pi\)). Then match \(c0,c1,c2,c3\) exactly as in (1). ✅

### 5. Candidate 4 plus \(c5\sin(Ac6+c7)+c8\)
Set \(c5=0\) and \(c8=0\), reduces to Candidate 4 which matches. ✅

### 6. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + c3 + c4\sin(Ac5+c6)\)

### 7. Candidate 1 plus \(c6\log(c7(c8+|A|)^{c9}+1)\)

### 8. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + c2 + c3 e^{c4 t}\sin(Ac5+c6)\)
The sine term in GT has **no \(t\)-dependent prefactor**. To remove \(e^{c4 t}\), either set \(c4=0\) (so factor is 1) or set \(c3=0\) (but then you lose the sine). Choose \(c4=0\). Also remove constant \(c2\) by setting \(c2=0\). Need zero phase: \(c6=0\) (mod \(2\pi\)). Then match coefficients: \(c3=0.4717...\), \(c5=0.8721...\), and exponential term via \(c0,c1\). ✅

### 9. Candidate 1 plus \(c5\log(Ac6+1)+c7\)
Set log coefficient \(c5=0\) and constant \(c7=0\) (and also the candidate’s standalone \(+c5\) doesn’t exist here; it’s \(+c7\) only). Then it reduces to Candidate 4/1 form; match as in (1) with \(c4=0\). ✅

### 10. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + c3\sin(Ac4+c5)+c6\log(Ac7+1)\)

The last term is \(c5\exp(c6\sin(\cdot))\), which cannot equal a linear sine term \(K\sin(kA)\) for all \(A\) unless it is removed. Set \(c5=0\) to remove it. Then remove extra \(A c2\) and \(A^{c3}c4\) by setting \(c2=0\), \(c4=0\). But then no sine term remains, so cannot match GT. ❌

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.3122*A*exp(-0.07984*t) + 0.4717*sin(0.8722*A)`

This has two terms:
1. `A*exp(c*t)` term (with negative coefficient and negative exponent coefficient)
2. `sin(c*A)` term (note: no phase shift, no constant offset)

Let me analyze each candidate by checking if extra terms can be zeroed out and if the core structure matches.

**Key observations about GT:**
- It's `A*f(t) + g(A)` where f(t) = c₀*exp(c₁*t) and g(A) = c₂*sin(c₃*A)
- The sin term has NO phase shift (or equivalently, phase shift = 0)
- There is NO constant offset
- No other basis functions (no log, no polynomial in A beyond linear, no extra exponentials)

**Candidate 1 verdict: [MATCH]**
